linguas="af am ar as az be be@latin bg bn_IN br bs ca ca@valencia cs cy da de dz el en_CA en_GB eo es et eu fa fi fr ga gd gl gu he hi hr hu id is it ja kk kn ko lt lv mk ml mn mr ms nb nds ne nl nn oc or pa pl ps pt pt_BR ro ru rw si sk sl sr sr@latin sv ta te th tr uk vi zh_CN zh_HK zh_TW "; \
for lang in $linguas; do \
  dir=/tmp/rhythmbox/pkg/rhythmbox/usr/share/locale/$lang/LC_MESSAGES; \
  /bin/sh /tmp/rhythmbox/src/rhythmbox-3.2.1/install-sh -d $dir; \
  if test -r $lang.gmo; then \
    /usr/bin/install -c -m 644 $lang.gmo $dir/rhythmbox.mo; \
    echo "installing $lang.gmo as $dir/rhythmbox.mo"; \
  else \
    /usr/bin/install -c -m 644 ./$lang.gmo $dir/rhythmbox.mo; \
    echo "installing ./$lang.gmo as" \
	 "$dir/rhythmbox.mo"; \
  fi; \
  if test -r $lang.gmo.m; then \
    /usr/bin/install -c -m 644 $lang.gmo.m $dir/rhythmbox.mo.m; \
    echo "installing $lang.gmo.m as $dir/rhythmbox.mo.m"; \
  else \
    if test -r ./$lang.gmo.m ; then \
      /usr/bin/install -c -m 644 ./$lang.gmo.m \
	$dir/rhythmbox.mo.m; \
      echo "installing ./$lang.gmo.m as" \
	   "$dir/rhythmbox.mo.m"; \
    else \
      true; \
    fi; \
  fi; \
done

	  $(INSTALL_DATA) "$$d$$lc/$$f" "$$helpdir`basename $$f`" || exit 1; \
	  $(MKDIR_P) "$(distdir)/$$lc"; \

	  (cd "$(dir $@)" && \

	  done; \
	  done; \
	  done; \
	  done; \
	  echo "$(INSTALL_DATA) $$d$$f $$helpdir`basename $$f`"; \

	  echo "rm -f $$helpdir`basename $$f`"; \
	  echo "rm -f $$helpdir`basename $$f`"; \
	  else \
	  fi; \
	  for file in $(HELP_FILES); do \

	  if ! test -d "$$helpdir"; then $(mkinstalldirs) "$$helpdir"; fi; \
	  if ! test -d "$$helpdir"; then $(mkinstalldirs) "$$helpdir"; fi; \
	  if test "x$(_HELP_V)" = "x0"; then echo "  GEN    $${po}"; fi; \
	  if test -d "$$lc"; \
	  if test -f "$$f"; then d=; else d="$(srcdir)/"; fi; \
	  if test -f "$$lc/$$f"; then d=; else d="$(srcdir)/"; fi; \
	  lc=`dirname "$$f"`; lc=`basename "$$lc"`; \

	  rm -f "$$helpdir`basename $$f`"; \
	  rm -f "$$helpdir`basename $$f`"; \
	$(AM_V_GEN) $(GLIB_COMPILE_SCHEMAS) --strict --dry-run $(addprefix --schema-file=,$(gsettings__enum_file)) --schema-file=$< && mkdir -p $(@D) && touch $@
	$(AM_V_GEN) glib-mkenums --comments '\'''\'' --fhead "" --vhead "  <@type@ id='\''$(gsettings_ENUM_NAMESPACE).@EnumName@'\''>" --vprod "    " --vtail "  " --ftail "" $^ > $@.tmp && mv $@.tmp $@
	$(AM_V_GEN)if ! test -f "$@"; then \
	$(AM_V_GEN)if test -d "C"; then d=; else d="$(srcdir)/"; fi; \
	$(AM_V_GEN)msgfmt -o "$@" "$<"

	$(ITSTOOL) -o "$@" $(foreach f,$(_HELP_C_FILES),"$${d}$(f)")
	$(_HELP_LC_VERBOSE)if test -d "C"; then d="../"; else d="$(abs_srcdir)/"; fi; \
	(cd "$(dir $@)" && $(ITSTOOL) -m "$${mo}" $(foreach f,$(_HELP_C_FILES),$${d}/$(f))) && \
	@$(NORMAL_INSTALL)
	@$(NORMAL_UNINSTALL)
	@for f in $(HELP_MEDIA); do \

	@list='\''$(gsettings_SCHEMAS) $(gsettings__enum_file)'\''; test -n "$(gsettingsschemadir)" || list=; \
	cd "$(DESTDIR)$(gsettingsschemadir)" && rm -f $$files
	done
	done

	done

	echo " ( cd '\''$(DESTDIR)$(gsettingsschemadir)'\'' && rm -f" $$files ")"; \
	else \
	fi
	fi
	files=`for p in $$list; do echo $$p; done | sed -e '\''s|^.*/||'\''`; \
	for lc in C $(_HELP_LINGUAS); do \
	for lc in C $(_HELP_LINGUAS); do for f in $(HELP_FILES); do \
	if test -f "$${mo}"; then mo="../$${mo}"; else mo="$(abs_srcdir)/$${mo}"; fi; \

	mo="$(dir $@)$(patsubst %/$(notdir $@),%,$@).mo"; \
	rm -f $(_HELP_LC_FILES) $(_HELP_LC_STAMPS) $(_HELP_MOFILES)

	test -n "$$files" || exit 0; \
	test -n "$(GSETTINGS_DISABLE_SCHEMAS_COMPILE)$(DESTDIR)" || $(GLIB_COMPILE_SCHEMAS) $(gsettingsschemadir)
	touch "$@"
$(_HELP_LC_FILES): $(_HELP_LINGUAS)

'
